<Text>Summary: Because of the grand review on Yelp I decided to give Hi Tofu a try. This place was a little hard to find, it was tuck in the corner somewhat on the side of La Cocina Restaurant.

Foods: Korean Style Veggie Pancake, Hot Stone Bibimbap, and a spicy Seafood Soondubu (which according to Hi Tofu Menu is just: Tofu Soup).

The Veggie Pancake was very bland and oily, I don't understand how the reviewer speak so highly of it. The sauce for the Bibimbap was a non spicy flavorless paste and anyone with experiences should know that the sauce is the main ingredient which completes the Bibimbap dish. As for the Soondubu (or Tofu Soup), I was devastated. The silken tofu was completely unseasoned and uncooked, which is... unacceptable. And why were there jalapenos in my Soondubu? If you call this place you run authentic then you shouldn't be adding JALAPENOS.

Service: The old lady (whom I assume is the owner/relative) was very kind at first but became hostile when I told her how the cook should use less oil for the pancake, jalapeno should not be in the soondubu, and the kimchi should be fermented a bit longer.

Overall: Maybe, just maybe when I can no longer drive myself to Korea Town in Orange County, I'll give this place another try. But for now, I'll stick with Kaju in Garden Grove as my go to authentic korean food.<//Text><pictures>None</pictures>< resp>
None< /resp>

I wore this two times because I am athletic and in the pool daily so could only wear it going out. I purchased this expensive item for my birthday in August 2020. It‚Äôs 7 months old. I requested a replacement and communication with this company once it was received at the repair center of theirs. I only received an email confirming that they got it back. No calls at all, holding onto a very expensive item of mine with zero communication and resolution. I was planning on buying the same bracelet in 18k gold this year but based upon this experience, I would never purchase again from Tiffany-it‚Äôs hugely expensive and at the very least they should offer impeccable customer care and they really don‚Äôt through the 800 number. Going into the store is great but getting things done through corporate and their 800 service is such a joke. They are the most expensive game in town-they should do better.

I visited Tiffany to purchase a necklace as a christmas gift, and my experience here was not an enjoyable one. Upon asking to see the necklace I had in mind, the woman helping me, rather than allowing me to see it the first time I asked, told me the price instead, hinting I may not have the sufficient funds to purchase it. <review>Referred here by a coworker. I was hesitant at first, as I am extremely picky about my barber. I ordered a bed frame in Dec 2019. The salesman in the store paired the wrong bed frame and headboard in the order, so when the bed arrived it couldn't be assembled. A technician who came to fix it thought the wrong screws had been delivered, so ordered them -- from the factory in Wisconsin.. 10 days to arrive, and when they did, of course did not solve the problem. When I complained a different tech ordered a new set of legs, --another 10 days to arrive, and again did not solve the problem.
At each visit to the store I was asked to wait at the customer service while a ticket was opened. Talked to the manager in person, and he couldn't help. The staff in the store seemed confused and kept passing the buck around about whose fault it was -- the factory in Wisconsin, the store etc.
After 2 months, the root cause was finally identified when they reviewed the original order. Then a new headboard was ordered --again 10 days to deliver. Finally got the bed set up in March 2020 --  3 months after the delivery!. No apology from the manager.

I observed the way the staff behaved during the whole episode -- the ladies at the front desk genuinely tried to help, but were hamstrung by their order process. The manager and other staff  could not identify the problem for a long time, and their discussions indicated they were just trying to point fingers.

Will never visit this location again.<//text>

The furniture and sets in the store are high quality, the prices are a bit high, but the service was so bad that it prompted me to leave such a poor review.  I would give 0 stars if I could simply because what I paid for has yet to even been delivered to me as agreed.

I ordered a table from this location on October 6th.  The rep was kind enough and fairly straight forward, though very slow (it took 30 minutes for him to fill out my information on the computer).  He told me delivery for Monday, the 8th.  I paid the cost of the table and the delivery fee, and signed the receipt and agreement, happy with the delivery time frame.  But an error occurred (gonna guess this was the fault of the technologically challenged rep) and the order had to be placed again.

After a few more minutes, the order was placed again - however now the delivery, told to me by rep and manager, was set for Wednesday the 10th.  Fine, not too bad - I leave.  Fast forward to Wednesday - no call, no delivery, nothing.  I look up my order and turns out it was actually set for Friday the 12th.  I am irritated at this point.

Come Friday, I'm taking time off work for this delivery yet - no call, no delivery.  I call the delivery center - they say that the truck tried to call me but could not get an answer (I received no calls).  After some investigation with the delivery rep, I found out the original store rep placed the wrong phone number in the computer.  It was CORRECT on my agreement and receipt, but he entered it WRONG on the computer.

After some time on hold with the store manager, I was able to get a measly refunded delivery fee and following Tuesday delivery.  Ideally, this store should have discounted my purchase as well, as I could simply charge back my credit card for 'no goods received as agreed'.  Because this situation is just that: my agreed upon delivery that I signed and paid for was three times dishonored, and I have yet to see my order.  On top of all this, I lost time from work to wait for this.

Please do yourself a favor and look elsewhere for your furniture.</review>
